  1. DOWNLOADS NEEDED:  
     - **C Compiler:**

       - Alternatively, Clang compiler (for static analysis with `scan-build` and sanitizer builds)

     - **Swift Compiler and Tools:**  
       - Swift toolchain version 5.0 or higher (to support `Package.swift` build configuration)  
       - Swift Package Manager (SPM) included with Swift toolchain for building Swift packages  
     - **Build Tools:**  
       - GNU Make (for Unix-like systems)  
       - CMake (for cmake builds)  
       - Ninja build system (optional, for cmake Ninja generator and Meson builds)  
       - Meson build system and Ninja (for Meson builds)  
       - Docker (version 28.3.2 confirmed, supports BuildKit and docker buildx, no GPU support needed)  
         - Use AMD64 Linux base images compatible with x86_64 (e.g., Alpine, Ubuntu, Debian) for container builds  
         - Do not include NVIDIA or GPU runtime components or flags in Dockerfiles or build commands  
       - Snapcraft (for building and packaging snaps)  
         - Install Snapcraft from official sources or system package manager  
         - Requires `snapd` and snap environment on Linux hosts supporting snap packaging  
     - **Package Managers (optional):**  
       - VCPKG (for Windows and cross-platform package management, optional)  
       - Conan (for dependency management and binary installation, optional)  
     - **Additional Tools:**  
       - Python (optional, if running test scripts, CI scripts, or fuzzers that require it)  
       - Git (to clone repositories and submodules)  
       - Clang’s `scan-build` tool for static analysis (optional but recommended for development)  
       - Valgrind (for memory debugging and CI medium and long tests)  
       - Sanitizers support in compiler toolchains:  
         - UBSan (Undefined Behavior Sanitizer)  
         - ASan (Address Sanitizer)  
         - MSan (Memory Sanitizer)  
         - TSan (Thread Sanitizer)  
       - QEMU user-static and system emulators for ARM, AArch64, PowerPC, PPC64 architectures available for cross-architecture testing and fuzzing if desired, but not required for native x86_64 build and test  
       - Docker CLI and daemon for building and running containerized `zstd` binaries via the provided `Dockerfile` (AMD64 base images only)  
       - Web browser or markdown viewer to read documentation files including `CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md`, `CONTRIBUTING.md`, `SECURITY.md`, `TESTING.md`  
       - **Shell environment supporting file descriptor manipulation** (e.g., `bash` or compatible shell) to support redirection features used in test environment initialization (e.g., `exec 9>&2`)  
     - **Operating System:**  
       - Linux x86_64 (Ubuntu 24.04 or Debian tested), with Docker and Snapcraft support for containerized and snap workflows

  current progress  
  - Base Ubuntu 24.04 image with required packages installed (gcc, clang, make, cmake, ninja, meson, git, valgrind, qemu, python3, snapd, docker.io, bash, curl, ca-certificates)

  - Snapcraft installed via snapd  
  - Docker group and user created for permissions  
  - Repository cloned and submodules initialized  
  - Default make build executed  
  - Tool versions checked  
  - Swift installation step fails during Docker build due to HTTP 404 error (exit code 22) when downloading the Swift toolchain tarball from the constructed URL  
  - Dockerfile uses environment variables in RUN command incorrectly (uses && instead of setting environment variables) which leads to failure in fetching Swift tarball  
  next step  
  - Correct the Swift installation RUN command to properly set environment variables and use them in the URL, e.g.:  
    ```Dockerfile  
    ENV SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3  
    ENV SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu24.04  
    RUN curl -fsSL https://swift.org/builds/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-release/${SWIFT_PLATFORM}/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE/${SWIFT_PLATFORM}-swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE.tar.gz -o swift.tar.gz && \  
        tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \  
        rm swift.tar.gz && \  
        ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift  
    ```  
  - Verify that the constructed URL is correct and the Swift version and platform exist on swift.org (consider checking availability for ubuntu24.04 or use ubuntu22.04 if ubuntu24.04 is not yet available)  
  - Optionally test the Swift download URL independently outside Docker to confirm availability  
  - Update Dockerfile accordingly and rebuild to fix Swift installation failure  
  - After successful Swift installation, continue with remaining build and verification steps as per plan

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install latest stable Swift 5.x toolchain for Linux AMD64
  RUN SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 && \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu24.04 && \
      curl -fsSL https://swift.org/builds/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-release/${SWIFT_PLATFORM}/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE/${SWIFT_PLATFORM}-swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE.tar.gz -o swift.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  # Install snapcraft from snapd
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  # Assuming the repo URL is provided as build argument or will be mounted externally
  # For example, build with --build-arg REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional, can be removed if not needed)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && scan-build --version || echo "scan-build not installed" && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  # Set bash as default shell and start interactive shell in /workspace
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

     - **Swift Compiler and Tools:**  
       - Swift toolchain version 5.0 or higher (to support `Package.swift` build configuration)  
       - Swift Package Manager (SPM) included with Swift toolchain for building Swift packages  
     - **Build Tools:**  
       - GNU Make (for Unix-like systems)  
       - CMake (for cmake builds)  
       - Ninja build system (optional, for cmake Ninja generator and Meson builds)  
       - Meson build system and Ninja (for Meson builds)  
       - Docker (version 28.3.2 confirmed, supports BuildKit and docker buildx, no GPU support needed)

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-22.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install latest stable Swift 5.x toolchain for Linux AMD64 using ubuntu-22.04 platform
  RUN curl -fsSL https://swift.org/builds/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-release/${SWIFT_PLATFORM}/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE/${SWIFT_PLATFORM}-swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE.tar.gz -o swift.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  # Install snapcraft from snapd
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  # Assuming the repo URL is provided as build argument or will be mounted externally
  # For example, build with --build-arg REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional, can be removed if not needed)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && scan-build --version || echo "scan-build not installed" && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  # Set bash as default shell and start interactive shell in repository root
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 3 ---

      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional, can be removed if not needed)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 4 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-22.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Corrected Swift toolchain download URL for 5.9.3 ubuntu-22.04 based on official swift.org archive path
  RUN SWIFT_URL=https://download.swift.org/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-release/ubuntu-22.04/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE/swift-${SWIFT_VERSION}-RELEASE-ubuntu-22.04.tar.gz && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 3 --retry-delay 5 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  # Install snapcraft from snapd
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional, can be removed if not needed)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 6 ---

      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Use the official Swift 5.9.3 Ubuntu 24.04 snapshot URL based on swift.org archive
  RUN SWIFT_URL=https://download.swift.org/swift-5.9.3-release/ubuntu-24.04/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE-ubuntu-24.04.tar.gz && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 3 --retry-delay 5 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  # Install snapcraft from snapd
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional, can be removed if not needed)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 7 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-24.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Download and install Swift 5.9.3 for ubuntu-24.04
  RUN SWIFT_URL=https://download.swift.org/swift-5.9.3-release/ubuntu-24.04/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE-ubuntu-24.04.tar.gz && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 3 --retry-delay 5 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  # Install snapcraft from snapd
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 9 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-24.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Download and install Swift 5.9.3 for ubuntu-24.04 (corrected URL and added curl verbose for debugging)
  RUN SWIFT_URL=https://download.swift.org/swift-5.9.3-release/ubuntu-24.04/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE-ubuntu-24.04.tar.gz && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 3 --retry-delay 5 --connect-timeout 15 --max-time 300 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  # Install snapcraft from snapd
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-22.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Download and install Swift 5.9.3 for ubuntu-22.04 (adjusted platform to a valid URL)
  RUN SWIFT_URL=https://download.swift.org/swift-5.9.3-release/ubuntu-22.04/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE-ubuntu-22.04.tar.gz && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 3 --retry-delay 5 --connect-timeout 15 --max-time 300 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  # Install snapcraft from snapd
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  # Configure Docker CLI and daemon permissions
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  # Clone repository and initialize submodules
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Build default make target
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  # Verify tool versions (optional)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 12 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-22.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN SWIFT_URL="https://download.swift.org/swift-5.9.3-release/ubuntu-22.04/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE-ubuntu22.04.tar.gz" && \
      echo "Downloading Swift from $SWIFT_URL" && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 3 --retry-delay 5 --connect-timeout 15 --max-time 300 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz
  RUN tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 14 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-22.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN SWIFT_URL="https://download.swift.org/swift-5.9.3-release/ubuntu-22.04/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE-ubuntu22.04.tar.gz" && \
      echo "Downloading Swift from $SWIFT_URL" && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 5 --retry-delay 5 --connect-timeout 15 --max-time 300 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz
  RUN tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 15 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-22.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN SWIFT_URL="https://download.swift.org/swift-5.9.3-release/ubuntu-22.04/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE/swift-5.9.3-RELEASE-ubuntu22.04.tar.gz" && \
      echo "Downloading Swift from $SWIFT_URL" && \
      curl -fsSL --retry 5 --retry-delay 5 --connect-timeout 15 --max-time 300 $SWIFT_URL -o swift.tar.gz
  RUN tar -xzf swift.tar.gz -C /usr/local --strip-components=1 && \
      rm swift.tar.gz && \
      ln -sf /usr/local/usr/bin/swift /usr/local/bin/swift
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 17 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-24.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      snapd \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends swift && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN snap install core && \
      snap install snapcraft --classic
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version && snapcraft --version && snap --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:24.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      TZ=Etc/UTC \
      SWIFT_VERSION=5.9.3 \
      SWIFT_PLATFORM=ubuntu-24.04
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      gcc-14 g++-14 \
      clang \
      make \
      cmake \
      ninja-build \
      meson \
      git \
      valgrind \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      qemu-system-aarch64 \
      qemu-system-ppc \
      qemu-system-ppc64 \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      docker.io \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      curl \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-14 100 \
   && update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-14 100 \
   && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends swift && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN groupadd -g 999 docker || true && \
      useradd -m -u 1000 user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  WORKDIR /workspace
  ARG REPO_URL=https://github.com/facebook/zstd.git
  RUN git clone --recursive ${REPO_URL} . && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  RUN make -j$(nproc)
  RUN gcc --version && clang --version && cmake --version && ninja --version && meson --version && valgrind --version && qemu-arm-static --version && qemu-aarch64-static --version && swift --version && docker --version
  ENV ZSTD_BIN=/workspace/zstd
  ENV DATAGEN_BIN=/workspace/programs/datagen
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 19 ---
